# Deferred Inventory Гўв‚¬вЂќ Standing Index

**Purpose:** canonical register of every deferred epic, deferred story, and named-but-not-filed follow-on across the project. Single source of truth consulted at:

1. **Every Epic retrospective** Гўв‚¬вЂќ per [CLAUDE.md Г‚В§Pipeline lockstep regime](../../CLAUDE.md) and Г‚В§Deferred inventory governance, the retrospective MUST review this inventory against the closing Epic's new substrate / evidence / learnings; flag now-ready-to-reactivate entries to the next sprint-planning round.
2. **Every session hot-start** Гўв‚¬вЂќ `next-session-start-here.md` surfaces the inventory counts so the operator sees "don't overlook" context every session open.
3. **Story authoring** Гўв‚¬вЂќ when a new story spec names a follow-on (e.g., "15-1-lite-irene is a fast-follow after this story"), the author adds the follow-on to Г‚В§Named-But-Not-Filed Follow-Ons below.

**Maintenance:** update at (a) each Epic retrospective close, (b) each story closure that names a new follow-on, (c) any session-wrapup where the operator flags a new deferred item, (d) each forward-port pass on the hybrid migration branch (see Г‚В§Forward-Port Deferred below). Last refreshed: **2026-07-11** (**Slab 6 trial-experience bundle 3/3 CLOSED.** Slab 6.4 closed today after third-pass verification-only re-trace clean + operator Gate 5 dual-gate ceremony PASS via `scripts/operator/gate5_slab_6_4.py` 83 passed; Mary harvest-gate A18 disposition: leave as candidate. **First tracked trial UNBLOCKED.** Earlier same day: 6.3 + 6.5 CLOSED after second-pass verification-only re-trace `8b165e8` confirmed CLEAN. Prior 2026-04-27: Slab 6.2 formal close: `migration-6-2-promote-dependency-map-into-manifest` RESOLVED вЂ” manifest dependencies promoted; alias-drift A9 patch landed; Composition Spec В§12 known limitation #1 closed; Slab 6.3 + 6.4 + 6.5 trial-experience bundle UNBLOCKED. Slab 6.1 formal close earlier same day: `5a-2-production-graph-entrypoint-substrate-gap` RESOLVED, six Slab 6.1 close deferred-inventory entries filed, M5 condition #3 RESOLVED, migration verdict promoted to unqualified SHIP).

## DID Scorecard Leak Registry

<!-- GOVERNANCE SECTION вЂ” NOT a deferred-work entry; it NEVER migrates on entry archival.
     This is the SSOT for the OPEN DID scorecard leaks counted (line-anchored) by
     app.quality.signals.open_leak_count_signal and reconciled against `open_leaks` in
     docs/quality/project-quality-scorecard.md В§1.6 by the leak-count honesty pin.
     MAINTENANCE RULE: closing a DID leak == remove its did_leak line HERE **and** decrement
     `open_leaks` in docs/quality/project-quality-scorecard.md, IN LOCKSTEP (the honesty pin
     reconciles the two вЂ” editing only one goes RED). Do NOT tag leaks under their deferred
     entries: those entries migrate to the В§Closed Entries вЂ” Archived section on close, which
     the reader excludes, silently dropping the count while the scorecard is untouched. -->

The 5 open DID scorecard leaks. Each line's HTML comment gives its В§1.6 criterion, its DID leak number, and a pointer to the deferred entry that owns the underlying work (the registry decouples the *count* from those entries' lifecycles):

- did_leak: leg4-narration-fidelity-gate-precision-before-flag-on  <!-- [C3] DID Leak 1 вЂ” fidelity fence OFF by default; owner entry: ## Leg-4 CLOSE follow-ons -->
- did_leak: gary-export-llm-brief-to-page-matcher  <!-- [C2] DID Leak 3 вЂ” Gary export title-match determinism-pretending; owner entry: ## Named-But-Not-Filed Follow-Ons table -->

- did_leak: reading-path-fresh-naive-holdout-pre-trial  <!-- [C5] DID Leak 4 вЂ” reading-path uncalibrated, fresh-naive holdout OWED (cross-links Q3.4); underlying follow-on lives inside the p2-4b entry [[reading-path-fresh-naive-holdout-pre-trial]] in ## Named-But-Not-Filed Follow-Ons -->

## Named-But-Not-Filed Follow-Ons

- вњ… **RESOLVED 2026-07-17 as Story 42-6** (`42-6-g0s-runner-default-wake-sentinel.md`, done + dual-gate reviewed): per-run wake sentinel written by the CLI operator path (default ON via `--prewalk-settings-confirm`; `start_trial` function-default OFF keeps tests deterministic; env flag kept as OR override; opt-out preserved). G0S now shows by DEFAULT on operator-steered runs. Original entry retained below for lineage.
- рџ”ґ **`g0s-runner-default-wake-policy`** (filed 2026-07-17 by Story 42-5 review; RESOLVED by 42-6 вЂ” see above): the new pre-walk settings gate `G0S` is operator-woken via `MARCUS_PREWALK_SETTINGS_CONFIRM_ACTIVE` (default OFF в†’ traversed byte-identically, mirroring G0E/G0R). So the pre-walk confirm surface is NOT shown by DEFAULT on a real operator-steered run вЂ” the operator must export the flag. The operator's 42-5 requirement (RED priority) implies it should be the DEFAULT for operator-steered runs. Clean fix (dev-flagged): a per-run persisted wake sentinel (run-dir file) set by `start_trial` for operator-steered runs + read by both walks вЂ” NOT global `os.environ.setdefault` in start_trial (would leak into the 13 start_trial test files). **Reactivation: operator/party ruling on default-ON вЂ” likely immediate (it's what makes 42-5 fulfill the operator requirement by default). Priority HIGH.**
- вњ… **RESOLVED 2026-07-17 as Story 42-7** (rider R3): 9 stale `tests/unit/manifest/` pins refreshed to the live 52-node manifest (node count 45в†’52 with attributed history; gate topology counts DERIVED-from-live; gate-id/fold pins += G0R/G0S; golden schema fixtures regenerated additive-only). `tests/unit/manifest/` fully green (74). ### Story 40-1 green-light follow-ons (filed 2026-07-16 at the 40-1 green-light round, amendment J-4; spec = 40-1-cover-placeholder-hero-toc-provenance.md)

- вњ… **FILED 2026-07-16 as Stories 42-3 (standing readout) + 42-5 (pre-walk confirm gate)** вЂ” Epic 42 Operator Surface Next-Pass, green-lit 5/5 (`party-greenlight-post-trial-bc747b51-arc-2026-07-16.md`). Row retained for the toggle-table reference; direction may flip if the toggle set evolves.
- рџ”ґ **`hud-pre-run-settings-confirmation-surface`** (OPERATOR REQUIREMENT, Juanl, 2026-07-16, issued live during the off-books C1M1-P1 concierge run; **REAFFIRMED + EXPANDED 2026-07-16 mid production trial `bc747b51`**): ALL run toggles (~14вЂ“16: component selection deck/motion/workbook, preset, encounter-mode, llm-execution-mode realtime/batch, MARCUS_G0_DISPATCH_LIVE, MARCUS_RESEARCH_DISPATCH_LIVE, MARCUS_RESEARCH_DETECTIVE_LIVE, MARCUS_NARRATION_FIGURE_FIDELITY_ACTIVE, voice-direction, MARCUS_DECK_ENRICHMENT_ACTIVE, MARCUS_UDAC_ACTIVE, coverage-gate family, MARCUS_TRIAL_BUDGET_USD, treatment slots A/B + styleguide picks) MUST be (a) **standing-visible on the HUD for the whole run** as the current settings that define that run, and (b) surfaced at the BEGINNING of a real run as a settings-confirmation surface the operator can confirm or CHANGE before the walk proceeds вЂ” a requirement on BOTH the HUD and the app's flow of execution (pre-walk settings pause/card + continuous readout). ### gh-pages site self-maintenance follow-ons (2026-07-03; from the picker gh-pages build-failure arc)
Parent spec: [`gh-pages-site-maintenance-routine-spec-2026-07-03.md`](gh-pages-site-maintenance-routine-spec-2026-07-03.md). Trigger arc: `jlenrique/jlenrique.github.io` legacy Pages build fast-failed at the ~1 GB published-site cap (847.5 MB); manual two-pass prune brought it to 456.1 MB and eliminated the fast-fail. These make the hygiene automatic/durable.
- RIPE NEXT SESSION -- **`gh-pages-maintenance-routine`** (PRIMARY): retention-prune on publish (>10d, allowlist-protected) + pre-push size guard (fail-loud >900 MB) + verify-build-after-publish (poll pages/builds via shipped httpx, fail-loud on errored/timeout, degrade-to-WARN if token lacks Pages:read) + CONSOLIDATE the publish helper duplicated across `picker_publisher.py`/`chooser_publisher.py`/`storyboard_publisher.py`/`skills/gamma-api-mastery/scripts/gamma_operations.py` into one `app/marcus/orchestrator/gh_pages_publish.py` + standalone `scripts/utilities/prune_gh_pages_site.py`. Full spec + 8 dev-agent ACs ready. **Reactivation trigger: operator green-light next session** (operator-declared 2026-07-03). Workflow: `bmad-quick-dev` with party greenlight -> dev -> code-review, Marcus-first. Direction-stable (bounded-staging is the end-state). *Direction may flip if the site migrates to a different host.*
- **`gh-pages-actions-migration`**: migrate the shared site from `build_type: legacy` to `build_type: workflow` (GitHub Actions Pages deploy) -- bypasses the legacy build entirely, surfaces real build logs (legacy builds do NOT appear in the Actions tab), removes the 10-builds/hr soft limit, tolerates symlinks, and needs no PAT-to-build. Still requires the retention routine (artifact size cap persists). **Reactivation:** if legacy builds keep failing/timing out even post-prune, OR when visible build logs become worth the switch. *Direction may flip if legacy proves adequate once the maintenance routine bounds growth.*
- **`gh-pages-image-downsize`**: transcode/quality-cap published PNGs (0.6-2 MB -> WebP/JPEG <150-250 KB) in the publish path to slow growth (~9 MB/publish -> ~1-2 MB). Multiplies the runway before any size ceiling; composes with retention. **Reactivation:** alongside or after `gh-pages-maintenance-routine`.
- **`gh-pages-history-shrink`**: optional `.git` history shrink (BFG/filter-repo) if REPO size (distinct from published-tree size, which retention already bounds) becomes a problem. Risky, rewrites history -- **operator-gated**. **Reactivation:** only if repo-size limits (not published-site cap) start biting.

### Gamma instructions-channel cleanup follow-ons (2026-07-01; from the `gamma-instructions-channel-cleanup` dual-gate CLOSE вЂ” operator-surfaced from live runs)
Parent: `gamma-instructions-channel-cleanup.md` (done). The story carries three design decisions surfaced at consult: (1) `stylePreset`вЉ•`style` composition вЂ” today the free-text `style` is DROPPED when a non-`custom` preset is set (`_act.py:605-614`), so composing keywords into `style` alongside a preset is an empirical/A/B question; (2) content-vs-style-medium separation вЂ” pin the `keywords` field's semantic contract as STYLE-MEDIUM-ONLY so on-card content labels never leak into the image-style string; (3) preserve source-wins precedence over the styleguide base when composing into `style`. *Direction may flip if substrate evolves.*

### concierge-leg1a follow-ons (2026-06-30; from the Leg-1a 3-layer code-review)
- рџџЎ **`directed-voice-override-cannot-suppress-rhetorical-role`** вЂ” Parent: `concierge-leg1a-rhetorical-role-emission.md` (Edge Case Hunter Finding #2). Now that `rhetorical_role` is live on the role-derived seed, an operator `voice_direction_overrides` entry for a synthesis segment can REPLACE the role with another populated role but **cannot SUPPRESS it to `None`** вЂ” `voice_direction_annotation._overlay` (`:117-127`) skips `None` values, so an override of `{rhetorical_role: None}` is ignored and `contrast_emphasis` survives (and on a v3 run the `[slow]` tag still rides). This is consistent with the pre-existing None-suppression limitation for tone fields, and Leg-1a's scope is narrow (synthesisв†’contrast_emphasis only; no operator workflow yet overrides rhetorical_role per-segment), so it is NOT a Leg-1a blocker (party-ratified at CLOSE 2026-06-30). **Cleanup:** give the override tier a way to clear a role-derived `rhetorical_role` (e.g. a sentinel `"neutral"`/`"none"` rhetorical value the compiler treats as no-tag, or `_overlay` honoring an explicit `None` for an allowlisted suppress-key). **Reactivation trigger:** when an operator needs per-segment suppression of a role-derived directed read, OR when Leg-1b/role-widening makes multiple roles emit (raising the odds an operator wants to veto one). Direction-stable (additive override capability; never relaxes a gate).

- рџџ  **`directed-voice-slower-pace-value-underpowered`** вЂ” Parent: Step-7 / Step-6-A-live terminal demo (2026-06-28, live finding across 2 real runs, first-run-stands, NOT retried-to-green). The roleв†’voice map resolves `pace=slower` to ElevenLabs `speed=0.94`, which does NOT reliably lengthen a clip vs `neutral` (speed=1.0): two identical-text neutral clips already differ by ~0.42s, and the 0.94 effect is swamped by that per-render nondeterminism floor. Worse, the В§F.1 `PEDAGOGICAL_ROLE_TO_VOICE` map only ever emits `slower`/`neutral` (worked_example/synthesis/assessmentв†’slower; definition/motivation/practiceв†’neutral) вЂ” **no `pedagogical_role` maps to `faster`**, and `faster` (speedв‰€1.1) was the ONLY pace pole that audibly separated in the Step-5 acoustic audition. Net: Consumer-A role-driven narration delivery is wired correctly and the role-differentiated settings ARE sent live and recorded in receipts (proven вЂ” synthesis/worked_example speed=0.94 vs definition speed=1.00, distinct request IDs), but its AUDIBLE role-differentiation is underpowered with the current frozen table. The CONTRACT + wiring are DONE + live-proven; this is value-tuning for audibility, not a pipeline defect. **Action (tuning, party-reviewed before applying вЂ” re-audition with the MUR-4 acoustic judge after):** (1) lower the `slower` speed (e.g. 0.85) for a perceptible slowdown; AND/OR (2) map a role to `faster` (e.g. practice/motivationв†’faster) so the audible pole actually fires; AND/OR (3) add a prosody/stability dial so role-delivery differs audibly beyond duration. Reuse already-captured Step-7 clips offline before any new ElevenLabs spend. **Trigger:** before relying on AUDIBLE role-paced narration in a shipped lesson. Sibling of `directed-voice-energy-scalar-and-best-effort-labeling` (both are "settings are sent but the listener-perceptible tell is underpowered" вЂ” a palette/value-tuning class). Direction-stable. Evidence: `evidence/p5-directed-voice-s7-terminal-descript-20260628T024652Z.md` + `...-s6-live-narration-aligned-20260628T024652Z.md`.
- рџџў **`directed-voice-energy-scalar-and-best-effort-labeling`** вЂ” Parent: Step-5 CLOSE party (Murat/Quinn-R/CD/Enrique, unanimous). MUR-4 PASSED on paceв†’duration (clean reliable tell); energyв†’broadband-RMS FAILED the 3Г—floor bar (О”0.0018 < 0.0099) вЂ” an honest measurement-PROXY finding, NOT a pipeline defect (the stability/style settings ARE sent per receipts; ElevenLabs spends them on timbre/prosody, not loudness вЂ” RMS is the wrong scalar). **Action (follow-on, NOT a same-run retry):** (1) re-measure energy with a perception-aligned scalar вЂ” integrated **LUFS / A-weighted loudness** + an **F0-variance / spectral-centroid** expressiveness proxy (Enrique: switch the SCALAR first; reuse the 5 already-captured Step-5 clips offline before any new spend; optionally then widen the energy palette separation); (2) add a **best-effort label** to the Storyboard B voice-direction panel for tone/energy (pace shown as the guaranteed dial). **Trigger:** next directed-voice iteration / before broader expressive product claims. Direction-stable. Evidence: `evidence/p5-directed-voice-s5-live-acoustic-proof-20260627T231354Z.md`.
- рџџ  **`p5-s2-role-seed-robust-source-to-final-slide-linkage`** вЂ” Parent: Step-6 (P5-S2) bmad-code-review (EDGE-1, HIGH, production-correctness). The narration role-derived voice seed currently joins the G0 card's SOURCE-corpus slide ordinals ("Slide 1".."Slide 6") to the FINAL deck's `slide_id` ordinals ("slide-01"..) **by ordinal value**. These are TWO DIFFERENT ordinal spaces: Pass-1 clustering splits dense source slides into sub-slides and RENUMBERS the final deck (a 6-source-slide deck becomes `slide-01..slide-11`), `ignore`-partition drops remove slides, and reorders shuffle them вЂ” so card-ordinal N в‰  final-ordinal N in general. **Shipped mitigation (conservative fail-open):** the specialist runs a DIVERGENCE GUARD вЂ” it applies role seeds ONLY when the source-slide-ordinal SET (threaded from the card) and the final-deck slide-ordinal SET COINCIDE 1:1; on ANY divergence (count mismatch / membership mismatch / clustering renumber) it emits NO seeds (neutral built-in), never a mis-seed. Voice is delivery-only so a fail-open neutral is harmless; a wrong-role seed mis-paces a real learner segment and is not. Consequence: in real Gary-generated decks (where the source's "Slide N" enumeration rarely equals the generated deck's slide set) seeding fails open and the feature is inert вЂ” it fires only when the source and final slide enumerations genuinely align (e.g. a preserve-the-source-deck run or a curated slice). **Durable fix (this entry):** replace the ordinal join with a CONTENT-GROUNDED linkage вЂ” match by component `source_ref`/content fingerprint в†” segment provenance, OR thread Pass-1's source-slideв†’final-slide cluster map (the authoritative split/drop/reorder record) into the projection so role seeds survive clustering. **Trigger:** when role-derived voice is wanted on clustered/real-Gary-deck trials (the current guard makes it a no-op there). Direction-stable (fail-open is the correct interim posture; the durable join only ADDS coverage, never relaxes the guard). Evidence/in-code: `app/marcus/orchestrator/enrichment_consumption.py` (`project_role_derived_voice_by_slide` NOTE) + `app/specialists/irene/graph.py` (`_role_derived_seeds_for_deltas` EDGE-1 guard). **вћ• Step-8 CF-A E2E finding (2026-06-28, Murat/Winston condition):** the fragility is WORSE than clustering alone вЂ” `slide_ordinal_from_locator` requires the narration component locator to TERMINATE exactly in `Slide N`, but live gpt-5 NON-DETERMINISTICALLY appends `> Narration` (~half of 5 live runs), yielding an unparseable locator в†’ the guard correctly fail-safes to NO seed. So even on a 1:1-aligned deck the voice-seed is non-deterministically inert depending on the model's locator formatting (it DID fire on trial `8a997d43` where the locator was clean: `by_slide={1,3,6}`). The durable content-grounded linkage must also be robust to locator-suffix variance (don't depend on an exact `Slide N` terminal). This gates a single-run all-in-one CF-A demo (where the ungrounded leg AND the voice-seed leg co-occur in one sampling); both legs are each proven on real runner runs today, just not the same sampling.
- рџ”µ **`directed-voice-adjacency-anti-jitter-audition`** вЂ” Parent: green-light (CD AM-6) + Step-3 CLOSE (CD). Storyboard B reviews each segment's direction in isolation; there is no cross-segment adjacency/jitter flag (e.g. urgentв†’reflectiveв†’urgent whiplash). Rubric В§4 frames coherence as an audition-bench concern, not a Storyboard-B gate requirement. **Action:** add a >1-step adjacent-dial-swing flag in the audition lane (Step 5) / a future Storyboard-B coherence pass. Non-blocking; per-segment review is complete + honest without it.

### P5 directed-voice arc вЂ” Step-9 NEXT-INCREMENT reactivation (2026-06-28; party Marcus/John/CD/Murat, UNANIMOUS, no impasse)

- **вћЎпёЏ REACTIVATED as the E bundle (next session, into a `bmad-create-story` chain вЂ” routing rec, not a substitute for the greenlight gate):** three already-filed entries graduate together into increment E:

  - **вћ• `seed` (from the В§10-item-5 sweep) is an INGREDIENT of E, not a competing increment** вЂ” graduate `seed` into the directed-TTS contract to collapse the ~0.42s render-nondeterminism floor that eats the pace tell (byte-identical determinism sweep-confirmed live; trivially RED-first hash-pinnable). **E success bar:** voice FIRES (not fail-open) on в‰Ґ1 real clustered Gary deck + Step-5 MUR-4 verifier shows a pace delta exceeding the seed-collapsed floor, cross-confirmed on a 2nd deck, AND **ear-proven blind A/B** (operator can't blind-call в†’ not cleared).

### P5-arc P2 (Texas pass-0) follow-ons (2026-06-26; from P2 design + T11 + party CLOSE)
- рџџЎ **`p2-pubmed-adapter-v2`** вЂ” Parent: P2 Texas pass-0 (`p2-texas-pass0-design-strawman-2026-06-26.md`; party R2 chose A5=scite-only-v1). scite's index has a coverage gap: a valid biomedical DOI NOT in scite's index returns the same `total:0` as a garbage DOI в†’ real citations mark `failed/not_in_index` (honest, never fabricated, but caps recall). Bare PubMed-URL citations (no DOI, e.g. slice `c014` `pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/31589283`) also can't resolve via scite. **Cleanup:** add a `pubmed` `RetrievalAdapter` (wrap the PubMed MCP tool; deterministic query/refine; `identity_key` DOI/PMID; `get_article_metadata`/`convert_article_ids` for bare-idв†’metadata). **Trigger:** when citation-resolution recall on biomedical corpora matters for a real (non-demo) deliverable. Direction-stable. Live-proven gap evidence: `evidence/p2-live-citation-resolution-2026-06-26.json`.
- рџџў **`p2-doi-multi-per-excerpt`** вЂ” Parent: P2 T11 (Edge-Case). `extract_doi` returns the FIRST DOI only; a second cited paper in one excerpt is silently dropped (DD4 models 1 resolution/component). **Cleanup:** per-DOI resolution rows when an excerpt carries multiple DOIs. Low priority.
- рџ”µ **`p2-universal-md-body-marker-collision-guard`** вЂ” Parent: P2 T11 (NIT) в†’ **P5 body parser**. The `<<<CLEAN_BODY>>>`/`<<<PROVENANCE_ANNOTATION>>>` demarcation is string-concatenated with no escape if a verbatim excerpt literally contains a sentinel. Add an escape/guard when the P5 body-splitter is built. Course content unlikely to trip it today.
- рџ”ґ **`p2-condition1-wired-live-run` + `p2-condition3-live-a4`** вЂ” Parent: P2 party CLOSE (Murat, BINDING). The one-process live `build_enrichment_result(dispatch_live=True)` must show BOTH `resolved` and `failed` in one live output, AND A4 `ungrounded` must be exercised on LIVE output. Blocked at P2 only by P1 gpt-5 extraction latency (resolver proven non-hanging; OpenAI responsive). **These RIDE THE FINAL-INTEGRATION E2E (which runs build_enrichment_result live anyway). If the final E2E skips them, P2 is RETROACTIVELY NOT-CLOSED.** Not a formality вЂ” a real gate. SSOT: `p5-arc-party-record-2026-06-26.md В§P2 PARTY CLOSE`.

> P2-1 backlink (2026-06-19): Quinn-R detector ratchet recorded in `docs/trials/cross-trial-learnings.md` under "P2-1 perception fidelity detector". **UPDATE 2026-06-20:** `fidelity-metric-blind-to-perception-regression` вњ… **STRUCK** вЂ” P2-1 (detector) DONE, P2-2 (PNG-perception) CLOSED, P2-3 (Pass-2 grounding fix) CLOSED + live AC-6 regression-green confirmed. Only P2-4 (reading-path, Growth) remains in the P2 arc, and it is enhancement (not the disaster-regression, which is now closed).

| **SciteProvider OAuth 2.1 migration + production-class MCP integration** (`5a-2-scite-mcp-oauth-integration`) | M3 ceremony probe 2026-04-27 in operator session; further-substantiated by 2026-04-27 heartbeat + ceremony successful end-to-end runs | **Candidate Slab 6.2 story** (paired with `migration-6-1-production-graph-runner.md` Slab 6 opener). Third A16 (Composition-vs-Component Audit Gap) instance surfaced when M3 ceremony attempted Scite MCP. Existing `skills/bmad-agent-texas/scripts/retrieval/scite_provider.py` is structurally wrong against the real MCP on **four** dimensions: (1) auth вЂ” hardwired to HTTP Basic but real MCP requires OAuth 2.1 Bearer per WWW-Authenticate header pointing at `https://api.scite.ai/.well-known/oauth-protected-resource`; (2) **tool count вЂ” assumes 3 separate tools (`search`, `paper_metadata`, `citation_contexts`) but real MCP exposes only ONE unified tool: `search_literature`** (verified 2026-04-27 via heartbeat + ceremony); (3) parameter names вЂ” assumes `query`/`max_results` but actual schema is `term`/`limit` plus 27 other rich filter params (year, journal, author, paper_type, retraction filters, smart-citation count ranges, etc.); (4) response shape вЂ” assumes per-tool result envelopes but actual response is `{total: int, count: int, query: str, limit: int, offset: int, hits: [{doi, title, authors, ...}]}` wrapped in MCP TextContent. Operator-session ceremony bypasses legacy `SciteProvider` via official `mcp` Python SDK's `OAuthClientProvider` вЂ” working reference implementation at `scripts/operator/m3_texas_ceremony_scite.py` + heartbeat at `scripts/operator/scite_heartbeat.py`. Live verified 2026-04-27: real scholarly results returned (53.8M-paper corpus; 5 papers per default query; DOI + title + authors per hit). | **Provider migration, ~5-6pt** (revised up from initial ~2-3pt estimate after 2026-04-27 findings doubled the migration scope). Update `skills/bmad-agent-texas/scripts/retrieval/scite_provider.py` to use OAuth 2.1 via `OAuthClientProvider`: (a) replace `auth_style="basic"` MCPServerConfig with OAuth-aware client construction (mirror reference impl in `scripts/operator/m3_texas_ceremony_scite.py`); (b) implement TokenStorage backed by repo-managed cache directory; (c) **collapse 3-tool assumption to 1-tool вЂ” replace `_SCITE_TOOL_SEARCH/PAPER/CITATIONS` constants with single `_SCITE_TOOL_LITERATURE = "search_literature"`**; (d) migrate parameter mapping from `RetrievalIntent` to `search_literature` schema (term, limit, offset + rich filters); (e) migrate response normalization from per-tool shape assumptions to actual `{total, count, hits: [{doi, ...}]}` shape; (f) live integration test gated `pytest -m live` exercising the unified tool; (g) deprecate `SCITE_USER_NAME` + `SCITE_PASSWORD` env vars (no longer needed for MCP); (h) ensure cross-validation with Consensus (per existing contract) still works given the unified-tool shape. ## Static-validation deck+motion+workbook findings (filed 2026-07-17)

Source: `_bmad-output/implementation-artifacts/static-validation-deck-motion-workbook-pipeline-2026-07-17.md` (independent read-only static validation). Triaged by Marcus-orchestrator 2026-07-17. **S-2 (G0 directive raw dump) is NOT filed here вЂ” it is OWNED by Epic 43 (HIL Surface Tabular Coverage), which supersedes and exceeds it** (43 fixes the systemic projector gap across all 13 gates, not just G0). - **`deck-plus-workbook-without-motion-catalog-path`** (S-4, MEDIUM, product question) вЂ” no catalog bundle for deck+workbook without motion; selecting workbook always forces the motion nodes. - **`section-11-display-voice-candidates-model-binding-mismatch`** (MEDIUM, VERIFY вЂ” surfaced by Story 43-4 dev 2026-07-17) вЂ” `app/gates/section_11/poll_surface.py` binds `display_voice_candidates` / `load_voice_selection` to `G4Card` (`from app.models.decision_cards.g4 import G4Card`), but the card that actually flows at a paused G4A `11-gate` (per on-disk evidence `.../s8-tejal-p4-terminal-walk-.../decision-card-G4A.json`) is a **`G4ACard`** carrying `voice_candidates` + `pick_context[].kind=="voice-options"`. `G4Card` looks like the fidelity-**closeout** model (artifact_paths/outcome_summary/final_status, `extra="forbid"`) вЂ” no voice candidates. If confirmed, `display_voice_candidates` is bound to the wrong model for the G4A surface (would fail/mislead on a real G4A pause). 43-4's renderer correctly targets the real `G4ACard` body, so this is NOT an Epic-43 blocker. - **`spoc-g0e-flagged-axis-diverges-from-projector-ungrounded`** (LOW / UX-clarity, SPOC-drift finding вЂ” surfaced by Story 43-11 parity test 2026-07-17) вЂ” the SPOC prose narration and the tabular projector surface DIFFERENT "flagged" axes for the SAME G0E enrichment data, so an operator reading both sees two different flagged counts. `app/marcus/cli/marcus_spoc.py::_narrate_g0_enrichment` surfaces the **`flagged_unconsumed`** axis: the inline per-component `[flagged: no generator today]` marker and the reconcile line's `n_flagged` ("flagged classification-only") вЂ” bc747b51: **13**. The projector (`hil_tabular_projector.py::render_enrichment_metrics` + `render_ungrounded_advisories`) surfaces the distinct **`flagged_ungrounded`** axis: `reconcile.n_ungrounded` ("Flagged ungrounded (advisory)") + the one-row-per-advisory table вЂ” bc747b51: **12**. The two sets are not equal (13 vs 12). Additionally the SPOC narration **never enumerates the ungrounded-advisory set at all** вЂ” the tabular `render_ungrounded_advisories` list has no prose counterpart. The 43-11 anti-drift parity test (`tests/unit/marcus/cli/test_spoc_projector_parity_43_11.py`) deliberately pins only the facts the two surfaces DO agree on (typed-component total, provisional/refined LO totals + LO identity sets) and leaves this flag-axis gap to this follow-on rather than forcing a risky prose refactor (43-11's lower-risk-default mandate). **Trigger:** when the SPOC G0E narration is next revised, decide whether the prose should (a) also surface the `flagged_ungrounded` advisory count/set for parity with the projector, or (b) keep the two axes but LABEL them distinctly so 13-vs-12 is never read as a discrepancy. Fix only on its own merits (SPOC-goal guardrail) вЂ” both fields are individually correct; this is a display-coherence choice, not a data bug.

**Probe finding (2026-05-19, post-Slice-D revert):** TW-7c-4's scope is **broader than the orchestrator and Round-2 party-mode appreciated**. The tripwire has TWO assertions: line 56 enforces `app_scope == []` (no `app/`-layer Python touches, which is the freeze condition everyone in Round 2 reasoned about); line 65 ALSO enforces `unexpected == []` against the full `touched_python` set вЂ” **forbidding ANY working-tree Python file change outside the 5-path `PERMITTED_PYTHON_DIFFS` allowlist**, regardless of directory. Slice D (`git rm tests/migration/test_slab_2c_next_session_start_here_updated.py`) fired the second assertion despite being a pure `tests/` deletion. Implication: **only edits to (a) non-Python files (YAML / JSON / Markdown / TOML / etc.) or (b) the 5 allowlisted Python paths are truly freeze-safe during pre-Trial-3.** This materially narrows the in-session housekeeping surface; most catalogued failures in `broad-regression-baseline-2026-05-07.md` require Python edits and are structurally blocked until post-Trial-3 substrate amendment.

| **`trial-3-blocker-section-02a-composer-not-wired-into-trial-cli`** | 2026-05-21 | **Root cause:** `app/marcus/cli/trial.py:17-18` imports `compose_directive` from `app.marcus.orchestrator.directive_composer` (the Story 7a.1 naive corpus-scan fallback with `DEFAULT_EXPECTED_MIN_WORDS = 200`), NOT from the LLM-driven `app/composers/section_02a/composer.py` (Story 7c.3a deliverable that closed Trial-2 finding #2). | **`trial-3-blocker-trial-cli-utf-8-launcher-wrapper-cmd`** | 2026-05-21 | **Secondary finding** surfaced during the same launch attempt: the operator launched the trial from `cmd.exe` (not PowerShell). The hot-start launch command prefix `$env:PYTHONIOENCODING="utf-8"` is PowerShell syntax; on CMD it returns "The filename, directory name, or volume label syntax is incorrect" and is silently no-op. Result: trial launched WITHOUT UTF-8 encoding set, re-introducing the Trial-2 finding #1 cp1252 crash vector for any Unicode-bearing corpus content. **Story 7c.2 was supposed to retire the operator-side workaround** by making the launcher UTF-8-safe by default; that closure clearly hasn't reached the CMD-invocation path. | **Fix scope:** make the trial CLI's main entry point (or the `_load_env_if_available` helper) set `os.environ["PYTHONIOENCODING"] = "utf-8"` and `sys.stdout.reconfigure(encoding="utf-8")` unconditionally before any I/O. ~5 LOC. Same substrate-amendment route. **Lower priority than the В§02A wiring fix** but should be batched into the same Sprint Change Proposal if both are addressed together. Test surface: re-launch from CMD without any env-var prelude; expect clean UTF-8 output even on Unicode-bearing corpus content. |

**Convergent disposition recommendation:** the existing 2026-05-19 SCP at `_bmad-output/planning-artifacts/sprint-change-proposal-2026-05-19.md` was a post-Trial-3 housekeeping motion. This Trial-3-blocking regression elevates it to a pre-Trial-3 binding amendment with extended scope. Either (a) extend the SCP В§4 to include the В§02A wiring fix + UTF-8 launcher fix alongside the original C1/C2/C3 phases, OR (b) author a NEW SCP scoped purely to Trial-3-blocking fixes and defer the SCP-2026-05-19 to post-Trial-3 as originally planned. Operator decides at next session start.

**Operator selected option (b) at 2026-05-21 session continuation:** narrow Trial-3-blocking-only SCP. New SCP file authored at `_bmad-output/planning-artifacts/sprint-change-proposal-2026-05-21-trial3-wiring.md` and party-mode-ratified (Round 1 4-of-4 APPROVE-with-amendments). Commits `12453bc..ab5562d` landed the substrate amendment + wiring fix + UTF-8 hardening + integration test. 2026-05-19 SCP remains queued for post-Trial-3 dispatch unchanged.

**Closure verdict 2026-05-21T22:00 re-launch (attempt-2):** В§02A composer was successfully invoked at G0; LLM produced a real-judgment directive (digest `351a57fb...`; size 4192 bytes; preserved at `state/config/runs/6a3393f8-f369-4a30-b7c1-b50c60c1d1a2/directive.yaml`, gitignored). Operator confirmed at G0 with verb `c`. Trial then halted at first specialist dispatch (Texas wrangler exit 30) вЂ” DIFFERENT defect class, schema-drift between В§02A output and Texas wrangler input. **The wiring fix worked. The integration boundary downstream is a separate Epic-scope issue filed below as `section-02a-downstream-consumer-compatibility-systemic-drift`.**

**Sibling entry `trial-3-blocker-trial-cli-utf-8-launcher-wrapper-cmd` also CLOSED 2026-05-21 via the same SCP (C2b commit `42ae4ec`):** trial CLI now invokes `_ensure_utf8_io()` at the top of `start_trial` to set `PYTHONIOENCODING=utf-8` + reconfigure stdout/stderr unconditionally before any I/O. CMD invocations work without the `$env:` prelude. Verified via 22:00 re-launch from cmd.exe.

## ~~CRITICAL Trial-3-blocking вЂ” В§02A composer downstream-consumer schema-drift~~ (filed 2026-05-21T22:30; CLOSED 2026-05-22)

**Status:** **CLOSED 2026-05-22 via Epic 34** (`migration-34-1-section-02a-wrangler-integration-roundtrip-test` through `migration-34-7-translator-deletion-anti-pattern-entries-epic-close`; commit range `bc477ed..1b59487`). Phase B Quinn-synthesis Option 5 ratified the integration-ratchet-first sequence; Story 34-1 installed the Section 02A -> Texas wrangler subprocess ratchet (bc477ed); Stories 34-2 through 34-4 harmonized the wrangler/schema substrate (cabf850 + 08dfc4a + 16e36f7); Story 34-5 pinned translator shrinkage (e59b0f4); Story 34-6 deleted the legacy composer (55a4d25); Story 34-7 deleted the temporary translator scaffold + filed A23/P5 anti-pattern entries + this closure marker (1b59487). Trial-3 attempt-3 is unblocked on fully harmonized substrate with no temporary translator and no legacy directive composer.

~~Second occurrence in the same trial-launch arc of "tested module, untested integration" defect class. The first occurrence (В§02A composer not wired into trial CLI) was patched via SCP-2026-05-21-trial3-wiring; the wiring fix REVEALED the second occurrence at the В§02A composer в†’ Texas wrangler integration boundary. **Operator-directed halt of Trial-3 attempt-2** at this finding (2026-05-21T22:30): rather than patch the symptom (one schema-drift gap) and risk discovering further gaps one-at-a-time, batch the full systemic fix.~~

**Observed at:** Trial-3 attempt-2 re-launch 2026-05-21T22:00 against `course-content/courses/tejal-apc-c1-m1-p2-trends/`. Run-id `6a3393f8-f369-4a30-b7c1-b50c60c1d1a2`. Operator confirmed `c` at G0. Texas dispatch raised `BundleDispatchError('texas wrangler reported hard error (exit 30); bundle not trusted')` from [app/specialists/texas/_act.py:323](../../app/specialists/texas/_act.py#L323).

**Root cause (verified by reproducing the wrangler subprocess directly):** the В§02A composer's `Directive` schema diverges from the Texas wrangler's expected input schema along multiple field/enum boundaries. Three known incompatibilities surfaced so far; more may exist deeper in the wrangler validation, and additional drift is likely at other downstream surfaces (Texas bundle в†’ Irene Pass-1, Irene packet в†’ В§04 G1, etc.) that this trial never reached.

| В§02A composer emits | Texas wrangler expects | Wrangler enforcement | Severity |
|---|---|---|---|
| `src_id` | `ref_id` | [run_wrangler.py:319-348](../../skills/bmad-agent-texas/scripts/run_wrangler.py#L319-L348) | Hard fail at validation; this is what crashed attempt-2 |
| `role: supporting` | `role: supplementary` | [run_wrangler.py:328-338](../../skills/bmad-agent-texas/scripts/run_wrangler.py#L328-L338) (allowed set: primary / validation / supplementary / visual-primary / visual-supplementary) | Would hard-fail on the next gate even after `src_id` fix |
| `role: ignored` | not in wrangler's allowed set | Same line range | Would hard-fail if any ignored source appears (Tejal corpus has none; dodged for attempt-2) |

**Forensic evidence preserved (gitignored; local-only):**
- `state/config/runs/6a3393f8-f369-4a30-b7c1-b50c60c1d1a2/directive.yaml` вЂ” В§02A-composed directive (sha256 `351a57fbe12aff4a49349c4a646618d92ae38a798ec53eee61668f74f8bbd703`; size 4192 bytes; 11 sources). Reference baseline for next-session diff comparison.
- `state/config/runs/6a3393f8-f369-4a30-b7c1-b50c60c1d1a2/run.json` вЂ” trial envelope at point of crash; `status: in-flight`, `completed_at: null`, `production_clone_launch_evidence_reason: registered-no-specialist-fired`.
- Reproduced wrangler error message: `[run_wrangler] directive error: sources[0] missing required field: ref_id`

**Why this is Epic-scope, not a one-line patch:** Story 7c.3a authored the В§02A composer as a fresh schema without verifying it conforms to **any** downstream consumer. The В§02A composer's own test suite (5 files, 12 tests) verifies the composer-in-isolation but never feeds output into the wrangler. AM-11 launch-permission token (52/52 GREEN) tests preflight + readiness fixtures, not end-to-end specialist dispatch. The Murat M-A1 wiring-contract test added in SCP-2026-05-21-trial3-wiring tests the adapter-to-composer contract but mocks `compose()` itself вЂ” it cannot detect output-shape drift. **Every В§02Aв†’downstream boundary is unprobed.**

**Resolution scope (Epic-level):**

**Phase A вЂ” comprehensive probe (~30-45 min next session):** Before any fix lands, audit ALL В§02Aв†’downstream integration surfaces. Targets:
- Texas wrangler input schema (this surface; surface more drift in the rest of `run_wrangler.py` beyond `ref_id` + `role`)
- Texas bundle output в†’ Irene Pass-1 input (does Irene read fields that the new wrangler bundle produces in a different shape?)
- Irene packet в†’ В§04 G1 decision card input
- В§04A per-plan-unit row schema
- В§04.55 run-constants lock structure
- В§07C storyboard build input/output
- В§11 voice-selection input
- В§15 final bundle output shape

Each surface gets a `grep` + `Read` audit; the result is a full integration-drift inventory (zero finding в†’ schema is clean; N findings в†’ batch into Phase B fix).

**Phase B вЂ” batched fix (1-2 sessions, scope-dependent):**
- **Decision point ratified at party-mode:** harmonize В§02Aв†’canonical or harmonize-downstream-to-В§02A? The В§02A schema is the NEWER authored deliverable (Story 7c.3a); the wrangler + downstream consumers reflect the pre-В§02A canonical. Honoring "newer schema is canonical" в†’ update wrangler + consumers. Honoring "minimize-blast-radius" в†’ revert В§02A to match the existing canonical.
- Either direction: requires substrate amendment (TW-7c-4 allowlist extension + lockstep test updates) via formal SCP route. Likely larger Epic than the wiring SCP (multi-file, multi-specialist).
- Consider authoring as an **integration-coherence Epic** via `bmad-create-epics-and-stories` with stories per affected surface.

**Phase C вЂ” closure (Trial-3 attempt-3 re-launch):** Once Phase B lands, re-launch from `course-content/courses/tejal-apc-c1-m1-p2-trends/`. Same corpus; same trial protocol. The Phase A audit + Phase B fix should de-risk additional integration-drift surprises within the В§02Aв†’downstream chain.

**Reactivation trigger:** immediate (next session is the BMAD sprint specifically dedicated to this Epic, per operator directive 2026-05-21T22:30: *"Start next session with a BMAD sprint to correct and address as many related issues as can be identified now and corrected proactively."*).

**Cross-reference:**
- Sibling-class finding: `marcus-interactive-experience-not-delivered-by-slab-7c` (Epic-scope; post-Trial-3 successor). That Epic is downstream of Trial-3 closure; THIS Epic is the gate before Trial-3 can re-launch successfully.
- Parent SCP (closes the wiring blocker that surfaced this gap): `_bmad-output/planning-artifacts/sprint-change-proposal-2026-05-21-trial3-wiring.md`.
- Pattern: this is the SECOND "tested module, untested integration" gap in the same trial-launch arc вЂ” worth flagging as a Mary-tier anti-pattern candidate for cross-trial-learnings.

| Entry | Filed | Trigger context | Resolution shape |
|---|---|---|---|

However: (1) the ONLY production caller of `emit_plan_lock_fanout` is `app/marcus/facade.py` (4A lesson-plan lane), with `tracy_bridge` an **optional kwarg the trial CLI never passes**; (2) `app/marcus/orchestrator/production_runner.py` contains ZERO references to fanout/bridge/Tracy; (3) the v4.2 manifest has no Tracy node, while Tracy IS in `CANONICAL_SPECIALIST_IDS` (roster of 12). Net: no tracked trial on the current substrate can exercise gap-fill research dispatch; Irene Pass 2 (В§08) proceeds on corpus material alone and the Epic-28 hard pre-Pass-2 gate (AC-S3) is vacuously satisfied because no Tracy dispatch ever opens. **Third instance of the A23/P5 "tested module, untested integration" pattern in the trial-launch arc** (after В§02Aв†’wrangler vocab fork and the resume-walker gate-pause gap). | **Resolution scope:** likely story-to-small-Epic, decided at retrospective. Candidate shape: (a) decide WHERE the lane attaches on the trial path вЂ” plan-lock at В§04.55 (G1.5-lock) is the designed trigger point per Epic 28; production_runner would need to invoke the fanout+bridge there (or the manifest gains a Tracy node between В§04.55 and В§08); (b) decide the operator-approval surface вЂ” the Marcus landing-point implies a conversational HIL stop, which couples this to the `marcus-interactive-experience-not-delivered-by-slab-7c` Epic (the Ireneв†’Marcusв†’Tracyв†’operatorв†’Texas loop is inherently conversational); sequencing the two together at architecture time is the natural move; (c) wire the AC-S3 pre-Pass-2 receipt check into the В§08 segment so the gate is real, not vacuous; (d) integration ratchet test FIRST per P5 (any Epic touching this producer-consumer contract starts with the green boundary test). **Direction may flip if substrate evolves** вЂ” if the Marcus-interactive Epic re-architects gate transport, the attach-point decision (runner-wired vs manifest-node vs conversational-lane) should be re-validated at dispatch, not executed blindly from this filing. |

**Cross-reference:** sibling-to and likely co-sequenced with `marcus-interactive-experience-not-delivered-by-slab-7c` (above) вЂ” both reactivate at the post-Trial-3 retrospective; the Tracy lane's operator-approval step is a concrete consumer of whatever conversational surface that Epic delivers. NOT blocking вЂ” single-workflow (narrated-lesson) trials run against the existing `state/config/pipeline-manifest.yaml`. This entry **consolidates three previously-scattered threads** so the capability is not re-derived each time it surfaces. Reactivation trigger: **operator-priority decision on a new content type** (same trigger as Epic 18-7), OR **post-Trial-3 retrospective**.

G4A DID carry real options in the specialist output (`enrique.voice_preview.voices` Г—3 with `sample_audio_url`) вЂ” they were just never projected onto `card.voice_candidates`. Operator's stated mental model: review the published Storyboard-A HTML, pick which of N variants per slide goes downstream; audition voices, pick one вЂ” and have the pick take effect. The substrate wired the pause+review+approve/reject skeleton but deferred enumerate-and-select. | **Resolution scope: Epic/large-story вЂ” the headline of the next trial series.** Three coupled pieces: (a) **produce real N candidates** вЂ” Gary double-dispatch (в‰Ґ2 distinct variant renderings per slide) surfaced into `G2BCard.variant_candidates`; enrique `voice_preview.voices` projected into `G4ACard.voice_candidates`; (b) **re-route on selection** вЂ” a downstream node reads `selected_variant_id`/`selected_voice_id` and binds that choice per slide/segment (the `edit` verdict's `edit_payload` becomes load-bearing); (c) **operator surface** вЂ” per-slide picker in the Storyboard-A HTML (couples to `marcus-interactive-experience-not-delivered-by-slab-7c`). Integration ratchet test FIRST per P5 (green pickв†’rerouteв†’downstream boundary before building). Likely co-sequenced with the Marcus-interactive Epic. |

## Production-envelope/bundle EXTRAORDINARY-ROBUSTNESS hardening arc (filed 2026-06-30; operator-emphatic architectural imperative)

- рџ”ґ **`bundle-carrier-extraordinary-robustness`** вЂ” owner: architecture (Winston) + Marcus orchestrator. The side-car that threads ALL workstream state вЂ” **`ProductionEnvelope`** (`app/models/runtime/production_envelope.py:100`, `contributions` + `add_contribution`) wrapped by `ProductionTrialEnvelope`, persisted as the bundle/run-dir (run.json/checkpoint.json/bundle_dir + g0-enrichment/segment-manifest/coverage-receipt/specialist outputs) вЂ” must be **EXTRAORDINARILY ROBUST** because every DEFERRED future consumer (enrichment, callbacks, lesson planning, multiple authored asset families) piles onto it; a weak carrier silently corrupts every downstream and the blast radius grows with each deferred feature. **Robustness contract (all required):** (1) schema-validated + `schema_version` + ADDITIVE-safe evolution (new field/asset-family never breaks an old reader); (2) append-only + `output_digest` provenance + first-wins idempotent re-dispatch (never silent-overwrite/drop); (3) FAIL-LOUD on missing/malformed/contradictory state (never silent-assume); (4) resumable + deterministic across pause/resume/recover with BOTH runner walks reading consistently ([[project-production-runner-two-walks]]); (5) single-SSOT вЂ” no shadow side-stores that drift (cf. the 5 scattered Gamma config stores, `gamma-styleguide-library-briefing-2026-06-30.md`); (6) new consumers read FROM the envelope in-graph (provenance > disk). **Shape (party-greenlit arc):** a carrier-coherence validator + schema-version/additive-evolution discipline + a fail-loud-on-corruption sweep + a contract test that a new contribution/asset-family round-trips through persistв†’resumeв†’recover without loss. **Reactivate:** before the deferred consumers (callbacks beyond Leg-1b, lesson-plan materialization, new asset families) attach in volume вЂ” harden the carrier FIRST. Memory: [[feedback_bundle_carrier_extraordinarily_robust]]. Direction-stable (additive hardening; never relaxes a fail-loud gate).

## gh-pages Publish-Hardening Arc Follow-Ons (2026-07-04)

Filed at the Task 4 done-signal party close (Winston/Murat/Amelia/John/Marcus вЂ” unanimous CONCUR-WITH-CONDITIONS; all five named the retry follow-on). Arc goal: `goal-gh-pages-publish-hardening-arc-2026-07-04.txt`. Evidence under `_bmad-output/implementation-artifacts/evidence/gh-pages-task{2,1b,3,4}-*`.

- рџџЎ **`gh-pages-publisher-bounded-deploy-retry-on-syncing-files`** (party-mandated close condition) вЂ” the durable Actions deploy path (Task 2) rides GitHub's `syncing_files` CDN stage, which flaked on **two consecutive** deploys this session (Task 3 cleanup `6dcc5dc`, Task 4 publish `0c6bf91`) вЂ” a stuck-rejecting streak matching the session-11 diagnosis (`picker-gh-pages-build-failure-diagnosis-2026-07-03.md`; external GitHub backend, NOT content/size вЂ” flakes even on healthy trees). Recovery today is a **manual empty-commit retrigger** (`f33903a`, `4950fac`). The publisher's verify-after-push correctly **fails loud** (never serves a dead URL вЂ” product-critical invariant; held twice against real backend failures), but an **unattended/autonomous SPOC production run would fail-loop + require an operator every time**. Shape: a **bounded in-publisher deploy-retry** on a `syncing_files`/deploy-stage failure BEFORE verify gives up (N retriggers with backoff), counted/logged, never masking a genuinely dead build; the operator browser Source-toggle/republish remains the hard reset. **Reactivate before any unattended/autonomous production publish run** (or when the operator wants to remove the manual-retry step). Direction may flip if GitHub's Pages backend stabilizes or the retention prune shrinks the served tree enough to drop the flake rate below relevance.
- рџџў **`gh-pages-served-tree-size-reduction-strategy`** вЂ” the retention prune shrank the served tree ~474в†’411 MB but did NOT eliminate the `syncing_files` flake (it fails on healthy trees too). If flakiness persists, consider a more aggressive served-tree reduction (shorter retention window, moving old proofing packs off the client site, or a dedicated Pages repo/site per the session-11 operator option) вЂ” an operator strategy call, not a code change.

## HUD Next-Pass Follow-Ons (filed 2026-07-13)

- вњ… **FILED 2026-07-16 as Story 42-4** (Epic 42 Operator Surface Next-Pass; depends on 42-2 lifecycle fix; own non-leak allowlist + identity-aware-access bar). The full requirement below is the binding spec for that story. Non-waivable activation trigger stands: build + validate before the next operator-steered production trial.
- **HIGH вЂ” `hud-stable-public-live-url`** вЂ” owner: HUD/runtime + publishing. The operator runs Marcus-SPOC on a one-monitor, always-online machine, so a full-screen local HUD obscures the working surface it is meant to support. Serve the authoritative HUD from localhost for minimum latency and full runtime flexibility, then expose it through an outbound secure overlay/tunnel; a permanent ISP address or inbound firewall opening is not required. **Ideal/operator-preferred path:** a named Cloudflare Tunnel plus Cloudflare Access on one stable custom hostname, reachable from any browser but restricted to the operator's approved identity. Prefer Cloudflare account login with MFA or an emailed single-use PIN allowlisted to the operator over a reusable shared/Basic-Auth password. Never use an anonymous quick-tunnel URL. **Acceptable home/private fallback:** Tailscale Serve with one intentionally stable machine name and `*.ts.net` HTTPS URL, accessible only to the operator's tailnet devices. Bind the HUD server to localhost, keep the tunneled surface read-only, require identity-aware access, and do not expose credentials/tokens, private source text, unsafe resume commands/nonces/digests, or other operator-only secrets. Preserve the full local HUD as authority. Couple lifecycle to Marcus-SPOC: run start launches/health-checks the HUD+tunnel, pauses keep them alive, and terminal status stops them after a short grace period. The named hostname remains reserved and stable between runs; when no run is active it may honestly show `HUD offline / no active run`. A fresh run takes over the same canonical hostname. No GitHub Pages deploy, stale snapshot, or high-availability layer is required for this operator need. **Non-waivable activation trigger:** build and validate this before the first production Marcus-SPOC trial directly steered by Juanl as operator/HIL; do not begin that trial with only the local full-screen HUD. Operator requirement: canonical location/name; newer run supersedes older run; URL remains stable. **REAFFIRMED 2026-07-16 mid trial `bc747b51`:** operator wants a **public, read-only page browsable from any computer**, ideally with an **unchanging URL**; local HUD also dropped at G0E pause (see `hud-lifecycle-survives-gate-pause`). Capture: [`evidence/operator-hil-display-requirements-2026-07-16.md`](../implementation-artifacts/evidence/operator-hil-display-requirements-2026-07-16.md).

- **HIGH вЂ” `windows-notifier-no-console-and-owned-child-cleanup`** вЂ” owner: HUD notifier/runtime test harness. During the 2026-07-13 Story-38.1 verification, production-runner tests repeatedly launched `python -m app.notify` for dummy trial `12345678-1234-4234-8234-123456789abc`. On Windows the `.venv` launcher delegates to the underlying `uv` Python, which acquires a visible `conhost.exe` despite `_detached_popen_kwargs()` using `DETACHED_PROCESS | CREATE_NEW_PROCESS_GROUP`; several notifier children outlived their pytest parent and continued showing empty terminal windows. Fix RED-first: launch notifier/watchdog truly windowless on Windows (evaluate `CREATE_NO_WINDOW` or `pythonw.exe` without breaking session-survival semantics), inject/fake the notifier in tests that do not need its real process, and guarantee owned-child teardown for every pytest fixture and failed preflight. Prove no visible console, no orphan child, one notifier per real trial, terminal-status self-exit, and unchanged logfile/watchdog behavior. Never terminate unrelated Python/notifier processes by broad name match. **Reactivate in the next HUD/runtime development pass; this is operator-visible and high priority.**
